msg:Environment: The hotel is at the gate of Beihai Silver Beach. The balcony of the room can see the beach, and the view is very wide. There is a small door next to the swimming pool that leads to the beach, which is public and free.

Facilities: The hotel is very new, the rooms are connected from north to south, the home decoration style is elegant, and the beds are thick and warm. The bathroom is separate, and the bathroom and bedroom are separated by blinds, which cannot seal moisture and noise. Fortunately, the air conditioning exhaust is powerful and there is no odor.

Hygiene: The indoor cleanliness is five-star. The fabric sponge sofa on the outdoor balcony cannot be sat close to the body and is damp for a long time.

Service: Half a day room fee will be charged after 12 o'clock until 6 o'clock in the afternoon. The front desk will call to urge check-out at 12 o'clock and 6 o'clock. The restaurant starts lunch at 11 o'clock. You can order dishes from the menu. Many seafood are not available and the dishes are ordinary.
Free parking in the underground parking lot.
